\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a48aea353b22e86deece00933ef941536}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-ticket\-\_\-parse\-\_\-t@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-ticket\-\_\-parse\-\_\-t}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-ticket\-\_\-parse\-\_\-t@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-ticket\-\_\-parse\-\_\-t}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-ticket\-\_\-parse\-\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef int mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-ticket\-\_\-parse\-\_\-t(void $\ast$p\-\_\-ticket, {\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-session} $\ast$session, unsigned char $\ast$buf, size\-\_\-t len)}}\label{ssl_8h_a48aea353b22e86deece00933ef941536}


Callback type\-: parse and load session ticket. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This describes what a callback implementation should do. This callback should parse a session ticket as generated by the corresponding mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-ticket\-\_\-write\-\_\-t function, and, if the ticket is authentic and valid, load the session.

The implementation is allowed to modify the first len bytes of the input buffer, eg to use it as a temporary area for the decrypted ticket contents.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\-\_\-ticket} & Context for the callback \\
\hline
{\em session} & S\-S\-L session to be loaded \\
\hline
{\em buf} & Start of the buffer containing the ticket \\
\hline
{\em len} & Length of the ticket.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, or M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-I\-N\-V\-A\-L\-I\-D\-\_\-\-M\-A\-C if not authentic, or M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-S\-E\-S\-S\-I\-O\-N\-\_\-\-T\-I\-C\-K\-E\-T\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-I\-R\-E\-D if expired, or any other non-\/zero code for other failures. 
\end{DoxyReturn}


Definition at line 1091 of file ssl.\-h.

\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a112d1fc2dd4db788592457d14c0c2899}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-ticket\-\_\-write\-\_\-t@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-ticket\-\_\-write\-\_\-t}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-ticket\-\_\-write\-\_\-t@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-ticket\-\_\-write\-\_\-t}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-ticket\-\_\-write\-\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef int mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-ticket\-\_\-write\-\_\-t(void $\ast$p\-\_\-ticket, const {\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-session} $\ast$session, unsigned char $\ast$start, const unsigned char $\ast$end, size\-\_\-t $\ast$tlen, uint32\-\_\-t $\ast$lifetime)}}\label{ssl_8h_a112d1fc2dd4db788592457d14c0c2899}


Callback type\-: generate and write session ticket. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This describes what a callback implementation should do. This callback should generate and encrypted and authenticated ticket for the session and write it to the output buffer. Here, ticket means the opaque ticket part of the New\-Session\-Ticket structure of R\-F\-C 5077.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\-\_\-ticket} & Context for the callback \\
\hline
{\em session} & S\-S\-L session to bo written in the ticket \\
\hline
{\em start} & Start of the outpur buffer \\
\hline
{\em end} & End of the output buffer \\
\hline
{\em tlen} & On exit, holds the length written \\
\hline
{\em lifetime} & On exit, holds the lifetime of the ticket in seconds\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, or a specific M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-X\-X\-X code. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a5695285c9dbfefec295012b566290f37}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-authmode@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-authmode}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-authmode@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-authmode}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-authmode}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-authmode (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-config} $\ast$}]{conf, }
\item[{int}]{authmode}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_a5695285c9dbfefec295012b566290f37}


Set the certificate verification mode Default\-: N\-O\-N\-E on server, R\-E\-Q\-U\-I\-R\-E\-D on client. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\-S\-L configuration \\
\hline
{\em authmode} & can be\-:\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-V\-E\-R\-I\-F\-Y\-\_\-\-N\-O\-N\-E\-: peer certificate is not checked (default on server) (insecure on client)

M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-V\-E\-R\-I\-F\-Y\-\_\-\-O\-P\-T\-I\-O\-N\-A\-L\-: peer certificate is checked, however the handshake continues even if verification failed; \hyperlink{ssl_8h_a516064f1468d459159ef7cd6c496a026}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-get\-\_\-verify\-\_\-result()} can be called after the handshake is complete.

M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-V\-E\-R\-I\-F\-Y\-\_\-\-R\-E\-Q\-U\-I\-R\-E\-D\-: peer {\itshape must} present a valid certificate, handshake is aborted if verification failed.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
On client, M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-V\-E\-R\-I\-F\-Y\-\_\-\-R\-E\-Q\-U\-I\-R\-E\-D is the recommended mode. With M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-V\-E\-R\-I\-F\-Y\-\_\-\-O\-P\-T\-I\-O\-N\-A\-L, the user needs to call \hyperlink{ssl_8h_a516064f1468d459159ef7cd6c496a026}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-get\-\_\-verify\-\_\-result()} at the right time(s), which may not be obvious, while R\-E\-Q\-U\-I\-R\-E\-D always perform the verification as soon as possible. For example, R\-E\-Q\-U\-I\-R\-E\-D was protecting against the \char`\"{}triple handshake\char`\"{} attack even before it was found. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a85c3bb6b682ba361d13de1c0a1eb69fb}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-ca\-\_\-chain@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-ca\-\_\-chain}}

Set the list of allowed ciphersuites and the preference order. First in the list has the highest preference. (Overrides all version specific lists) 

\begin{DoxyVerb}                 The ciphersuites array is not copied, and must remain
                 valid for the lifetime of the ssl_config.

                 Note: The server uses its own preferences
                 over the preference of the client unless
                 MBEDTLS_SSL_SRV_RESPECT_CLIENT_PREFERENCE is defined!
\end{DoxyVerb}



\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

With D\-T\-L\-S, use M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-M\-I\-N\-O\-R\-\_\-\-V\-E\-R\-S\-I\-O\-N\-\_\-2 for D\-T\-L\-S 1.\-0 and M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-M\-I\-N\-O\-R\-\_\-\-V\-E\-R\-S\-I\-O\-N\-\_\-3 for D\-T\-L\-S 1.\-2 
\end{DoxyNote}
\hypertarget{ssl_8h_ae1d705b8fc48224262ab92eb5aa4598c}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-curves@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-curves}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-curves@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-curves}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-curves}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-curves (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-config} $\ast$}]{conf, }
\item[{const {\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ecp\-\_\-group\-\_\-id} $\ast$}]{curves}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_ae1d705b8fc48224262ab92eb5aa4598c}


Set the allowed curves in order of preference. (Default\-: all defined curves.) 

\begin{DoxyVerb}            On server: this only affects selection of the ECDHE curve;
            the curves used for ECDH and ECDSA are determined by the
            list of available certificates instead.

            On client: this affects the list of curves offered for any
            use. The server can override our preference order.

            Both sides: limits the set of curves used by peer to the
            listed curves for any use ECDHE and the end-entity
            certificate.
\end{DoxyVerb}


\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This has no influence on which curve are allowed inside the certificate chains, see {\ttfamily \hyperlink{ssl_8h_a35fde8579e1be441445daa09f8c639ed}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-cert\-\_\-profile()}} for that. For example, if the peer's certificate chain is E\-E -\/$>$ C\-A\-\_\-int -\/$>$ C\-A\-\_\-root, then the allowed curves for E\-E are controlled by {\ttfamily \hyperlink{ssl_8h_ae1d705b8fc48224262ab92eb5aa4598c}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-curves()}} but for C\-A\-\_\-int and C\-A\-\_\-root it's {\ttfamily \hyperlink{ssl_8h_a35fde8579e1be441445daa09f8c639ed}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-cert\-\_\-profile()}}.

This list should be ordered by decreasing preference (preferred curve first).
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\-S\-L configuration \\
\hline
{\em curves} & Ordered list of allowed curves, terminated by M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-E\-C\-P\-\_\-\-D\-P\-\_\-\-N\-O\-N\-E. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

)}}\label{ssl_8h_ab15dcbe7c7fe2a5c118e7c486c07c921}

\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a46d919254eafef2ae642fb692c5e560a}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dtls\-\_\-anti\-\_\-replay@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dtls\-\_\-anti\-\_\-replay}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dtls\-\_\-anti\-\_\-replay@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dtls\-\_\-anti\-\_\-replay}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dtls\-\_\-anti\-\_\-replay}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dtls\-\_\-anti\-\_\-replay (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\item[{char}]{mode}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_a46d919254eafef2ae642fb692c5e560a}


Enable or disable anti-\/replay protection for D\-T\-L\-S. (D\-T\-L\-S only, no effect on T\-L\-S.) Default\-: enabled. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\-S\-L configuration \\
\hline
{\em mode} & M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-A\-N\-T\-I\-\_\-\-R\-E\-P\-L\-A\-Y\-\_\-\-E\-N\-A\-B\-L\-E\-D or M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-A\-N\-T\-I\-\_\-\-R\-E\-P\-L\-A\-Y\-\_\-\-D\-I\-S\-A\-B\-L\-E\-D.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Disabling this is a security risk unless the application protocol handles duplicated packets in a safe way. You should not disable this without careful consideration. However, if your application already detects duplicated packets and needs information about them to adjust its transmission strategy, then you'll want to disable this. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a9baa37a4b839319d00d8b43c8d266719}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dtls\-\_\-badmac\-\_\-limit@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dtls\-\_\-badmac\-\_\-limit}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dtls\-\_\-badmac\-\_\-limit@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dtls\-\_\-badmac\-\_\-limit}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dtls\-\_\-badmac\-\_\-limit}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dtls\-\_\-badmac\-\_\-limit (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-config} $\ast$}]{conf, }
\item[{unsigned}]{limit}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_a9baa37a4b839319d00d8b43c8d266719}


Set a limit on the number of records with a bad M\-A\-C before terminating the connection. (D\-T\-L\-S only, no effect on T\-L\-S.) Default\-: 0 (disabled). 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\-S\-L configuration \\
\hline
{\em limit} & Limit, or 0 to disable.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If the limit is N, then the connection is terminated when the Nth non-\/authentic record is seen.

Records with an invalid header are not counted, only the ones going through the authentication-\/decryption phase.

This is a security trade-\/off related to the fact that it's often relatively easy for an active attacker ot inject U\-D\-P datagrams. On one hand, setting a low limit here makes it easier for such an attacker to forcibly terminated a connection. On the other hand, a high limit or no limit might make us waste resources checking authentication on many bogus packets. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a5865631bc70b4511c25f558d5221fd65}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dtls\-\_\-cookies@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-dtls\-\_\-cookies}}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_a5865631bc70b4511c25f558d5221fd65}


Register callbacks for D\-T\-L\-S cookies (Server only. D\-T\-L\-S only.) 

\begin{DoxyVerb}             Default: dummy callbacks that fail, in order to force you to
             register working callbacks (and initialize their context).

             To disable HelloVerifyRequest, register NULL callbacks.
\end{DoxyVerb}


\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Disabling hello verification allows your server to be used for amplification in Do\-S attacks against other hosts. Only disable if you known this can't happen in your particular environment.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
See comments on {\ttfamily \hyperlink{ssl_8h_a4a37e497cd08c896870a42b1b618186e}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-handshake()}} about handling the M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-H\-E\-L\-L\-O\-\_\-\-V\-E\-R\-I\-F\-Y\-\_\-\-R\-E\-Q\-U\-I\-R\-E\-D that is expected on the first handshake attempt when this is enabled.
\end{DoxyNote}

\hypertarget{ssl_8h_abb5a878b9aabe137572a8c73a840c480}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-fallback@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-fallback}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-fallback@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-fallback}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-fallback}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-fallback (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-config} $\ast$}]{conf, }
\item[{char}]{fallback}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_abb5a878b9aabe137572a8c73a840c480}


Set the fallback flag (client-\/side only). (Default\-: M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-I\-S\-\_\-\-N\-O\-T\-\_\-\-F\-A\-L\-L\-B\-A\-C\-K). 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Set to M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-I\-S\-\_\-\-F\-A\-L\-L\-B\-A\-C\-K when preparing a fallback connection, that is a connection with max\-\_\-version set to a lower value than the value you're willing to use. Such fallback connections are not recommended but are sometimes necessary to interoperate with buggy (version-\/intolerant) servers.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
You should N\-O\-T set this to M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-I\-S\-\_\-\-F\-A\-L\-L\-B\-A\-C\-K for non-\/fallback connections! This would appear to work for a while, then cause failures when the server is upgraded to support a newer T\-L\-S version.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\-S\-L configuration \\
\hline
{\em fallback} & M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-I\-S\-\_\-\-N\-O\-T\-\_\-\-F\-A\-L\-L\-B\-A\-C\-K or M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-I\-S\-\_\-\-F\-A\-L\-L\-B\-A\-C\-K \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\item[{uint32\-\_\-t}]{max}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_a6625bc4e7ffd535900ef53259cc21651}


Set retransmit timeout values for the D\-T\-L\-S handshale. (D\-T\-L\-S only, no effect on T\-L\-S.) 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\-S\-L configuration \\
\hline
{\em min} & Initial timeout value in milliseconds. Default\-: 1000 (1 second). \\
\hline
{\em max} & Maximum timeout value in milliseconds. Default\-: 60000 (60 seconds).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Default values are from R\-F\-C 6347 section 4.\-2.\-4.\-1.

Higher values for initial timeout may increase average handshake latency. Lower values may increase the risk of network congestion by causing more retransmissions. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a193c7bf368780f485e20170c807709e5}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-legacy\-\_\-renegotiation@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-legacy\-\_\-renegotiation}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-legacy\-\_\-renegotiation@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-legacy\-\_\-renegotiation}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-legacy\-\_\-renegotiation}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-legacy\-\_\-renegotiation (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-config} $\ast$}]{conf, }
\item[{int}]{allow\-\_\-legacy}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_a193c7bf368780f485e20170c807709e5}


Prevent or allow legacy renegotiation. (Default\-: M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-L\-E\-G\-A\-C\-Y\-\_\-\-N\-O\-\_\-\-R\-E\-N\-E\-G\-O\-T\-I\-A\-T\-I\-O\-N) 

\begin{DoxyVerb}            MBEDTLS_SSL_LEGACY_NO_RENEGOTIATION allows connections to
            be established even if the peer does not support
            secure renegotiation, but does not allow renegotiation
            to take place if not secure.
            (Interoperable and secure option)

            MBEDTLS_SSL_LEGACY_ALLOW_RENEGOTIATION allows renegotiations
            with non-upgraded peers. Allowing legacy renegotiation
            makes the connection vulnerable to specific man in the
            middle attacks. (See RFC 5746)
            (Most interoperable and least secure option)

            MBEDTLS_SSL_LEGACY_BREAK_HANDSHAKE breaks off connections
            if peer does not support secure renegotiation. Results
            in interoperability issues with non-upgraded peers
            that do not support renegotiation altogether.
            (Most secure option, interoperability issues)
\end{DoxyVerb}



\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\-S\-L configuration \\
\hline
{\em allow\-\_\-legacy} & Prevent or allow (S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-N\-O\-\_\-\-L\-E\-G\-A\-C\-Y\-\_\-\-R\-E\-N\-E\-G\-O\-T\-I\-A\-T\-I\-O\-N, S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-A\-L\-L\-O\-W\-\_\-\-L\-E\-G\-A\-C\-Y\-\_\-\-R\-E\-N\-E\-G\-O\-T\-I\-A\-T\-I\-O\-N or M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-L\-E\-G\-A\-C\-Y\-\_\-\-B\-R\-E\-A\-K\-\_\-\-H\-A\-N\-D\-S\-H\-A\-K\-E) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a4e54e9ace21beb608bae36ddb81a4fb0}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-own\-\_\-cert@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-own\-\_\-cert}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-own\-\_\-cert@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-own\-\_\-cert}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-own\-\_\-cert}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-own\-\_\-cert (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-config} $\ast$}]{conf, }
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-x509\-\_\-crt} $\ast$}]{own\-\_\-cert, }
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-pk\-\_\-context} $\ast$}]{pk\-\_\-key}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_a4e54e9ace21beb608bae36ddb81a4fb0}


Set own certificate chain and private key. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
own\-\_\-cert should contain in order from the bottom up your certificate chain. The top certificate (self-\/signed) can be omitted.

On server, this function can be called multiple times to provision more than one cert/key pair (eg one E\-C\-D\-S\-A, one R\-S\-A with S\-H\-A-\/256, one R\-S\-A with S\-H\-A-\/1). An adequate certificate will be selected according to the client's advertised capabilities. In case mutliple certificates are adequate, preference is given to the one set by the first call to this function, then second, etc.

On client, only the first call has any effect.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\-S\-L configuration \\
\hline
{\em own\-\_\-cert} & own public certificate chain \\
\hline
{\em pk\-\_\-key} & own private key\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a1b804626a236e493316c58b048ab5937}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-psk\-\_\-cb@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-psk\-\_\-cb}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-psk\-\_\-cb@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-psk\-\_\-cb}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-psk\-\_\-cb}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-psk\-\_\-cb (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-config} $\ast$}]{conf, }
\item[{int($\ast$)(void $\ast$, {\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-context} $\ast$, const unsigned char $\ast$, size\-\_\-t)}]{f\-\_\-psk, }
\item[{void $\ast$}]{p\-\_\-psk}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_a1b804626a236e493316c58b048ab5937}


Set the P\-S\-K callback (server-\/side only). 

\begin{DoxyVerb}            If set, the PSK callback is called for each
            handshake where a PSK ciphersuite was negotiated.
            The caller provides the identity received and wants to
            receive the actual PSK data and length.

            The callback has the following parameters: (void *parameter,
            mbedtls_ssl_context *ssl, const unsigned char *psk_identity,
            size_t identity_len)
            If a valid PSK identity is found, the callback should use
            \c mbedtls_ssl_set_hs_psk() on the ssl context to set the
            correct PSK and return 0.
            Any other return value will result in a denied PSK identity.
\end{DoxyVerb}


\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If you set a P\-S\-K callback using this function, then you don't need to set a P\-S\-K key and identity using {\ttfamily \hyperlink{ssl_8h_a1e185199e3ff613bdd1c8231a19e24fc}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-psk()}}.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\-S\-L configuration \\
\hline
{\em f\-\_\-psk} & P\-S\-K identity function \\
\hline
{\em p\-\_\-psk} & P\-S\-K identity parameter \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a0d925033b3a46a48b3f8acc1d743af90}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-read\-\_\-timeout@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-read\-\_\-timeout}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-read\-\_\-timeout@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-read\-\_\-timeout}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-read\-\_\-timeout}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-read\-\_\-timeout (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-config} $\ast$}]{conf, }
\item[{uint32\-\_\-t}]{timeout}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_a0d925033b3a46a48b3f8acc1d743af90}


Set the timeout period for \hyperlink{ssl_8h_aa2c29eeb1deaf5ad9f01a7515006ede5}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-read()} (Default\-: no timeout.) 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\-S\-L configuration context \\
\hline
{\em timeout} & Timeout value in milliseconds. Use 0 for no timeout (default).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
With blocking I/\-O, this will only work if a non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L {\ttfamily f\-\_\-recv\-\_\-timeout} was set with {\ttfamily \hyperlink{ssl_8h_a143c1f887e1a2ca33b684ba4cf6c0543}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-set\-\_\-bio()}}. With non-\/blocking I/\-O, this will only work if timer callbacks were set with {\ttfamily \hyperlink{ssl_8h_a969d40f929829829e5196c6829220da7}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-set\-\_\-timer\-\_\-cb()}}.

With non-\/blocking I/\-O, you may also skip this function altogether and handle timeouts at the application layer. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\hypertarget{ssl_8h_aad4f50fc1c0a018fd5eb18fd9621d0d3}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-renegotiation@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-renegotiation}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-renegotiation@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-renegotiation}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-renegotiation}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-renegotiation (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-config} $\ast$}]{conf, }
\item[{int}]{renegotiation}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_aad4f50fc1c0a018fd5eb18fd9621d0d3}


Enable / Disable renegotiation support for connection when initiated by peer (Default\-: M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-R\-E\-N\-E\-G\-O\-T\-I\-A\-T\-I\-O\-N\-\_\-\-D\-I\-S\-A\-B\-L\-E\-D) 

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
It is recommended to always disable renegotation unless you know you need it and you know what you're doing. In the past, there has been several issues associated with renegotiation or a poor understanding of its properties.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Server-\/side, enabling renegotiation also makes the server susceptible to a resource Do\-S by a malicious client.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\-S\-L configuration \\
\hline
{\em renegotiation} & Enable or disable (M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-R\-E\-N\-E\-G\-O\-T\-I\-A\-T\-I\-O\-N\-\_\-\-E\-N\-A\-B\-L\-E\-D or M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-R\-E\-N\-E\-G\-O\-T\-I\-A\-T\-I\-O\-N\-\_\-\-D\-I\-S\-A\-B\-L\-E\-D) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a2d193b15941a556baaf2cb94138d66df}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-renegotiation\-\_\-enforced@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-renegotiation\-\_\-enforced}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-renegotiation\-\_\-enforced@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-renegotiation\-\_\-enforced}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-renegotiation\-\_\-enforced}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-renegotiation\-\_\-enforced (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-config} $\ast$}]{conf, }
\item[{int}]{max\-\_\-records}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_a2d193b15941a556baaf2cb94138d66df}


Enforce renegotiation requests. (Default\-: enforced, max\-\_\-records = 16) 

\begin{DoxyVerb}            When we request a renegotiation, the peer can comply or
            ignore the request. This function allows us to decide
            whether to enforce our renegotiation requests by closing
            the connection if the peer doesn't comply.

            However, records could already be in transit from the peer
            when the request is emitted. In order to increase
            reliability, we can accept a number of records before the
            expected handshake records.

            The optimal value is highly dependent on the specific usage
            scenario.
\end{DoxyVerb}


\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
With D\-T\-L\-S and server-\/initiated renegotiation, the Hello\-Request is retransmited every time \hyperlink{ssl_8h_aa2c29eeb1deaf5ad9f01a7515006ede5}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-read()} times out or receives Application Data, until\-:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item max\-\_\-records records have beens seen, if it is $>$= 0, or
\item the number of retransmits that would happen during an actual handshake has been reached. Please remember the request might be lost a few times if you consider setting max\-\_\-records to a really low value.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
On client, the grace period can only happen during \hyperlink{ssl_8h_aa2c29eeb1deaf5ad9f01a7515006ede5}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-read()}, as opposed to \hyperlink{ssl_8h_a5bbda87d484de82df730758b475f32e5}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-write()} and \hyperlink{ssl_8h_a49b7a27a616495d5f0a4fabc3f550dbb}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-renegotiate()} which always behave as if max\-\_\-record was 0. The reason is, if we receive application data from the server, we need a place to write it, which only happens during \hyperlink{ssl_8h_aa2c29eeb1deaf5ad9f01a7515006ede5}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-read()}.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\-S\-L configuration \\
\hline
{\em max\-\_\-records} & Use M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-R\-E\-N\-E\-G\-O\-T\-I\-A\-T\-I\-O\-N\-\_\-\-N\-O\-T\-\_\-\-E\-N\-F\-O\-R\-C\-E\-D if you don't want to enforce renegotiation, or a non-\/negative value to enforce it but allow for a grace period of max\-\_\-records records. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a1785faa0640bd6190c1c17a94b408e31}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-renegotiation\-\_\-period@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-renegotiation\-\_\-period}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-renegotiation\-\_\-period@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-renegotiation\-\_\-period}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-renegotiation\-\_\-period}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-renegotiation\-\_\-period (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-config} $\ast$}]{conf, }
\item[{const unsigned char}]{period\mbox{[}8\mbox{]}}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_a1785faa0640bd6190c1c17a94b408e31}


Set record counter threshold for periodic renegotiation. (Default\-: 2$^\wedge$64 -\/ 256.) 

\begin{DoxyVerb}            Renegotiation is automatically triggered when a record
            counter (outgoing or ingoing) crosses the defined
            threshold. The default value is meant to prevent the
            connection from being closed when the counter is about to
            reached its maximal value (it is not allowed to wrap).

            Lower values can be used to enforce policies such as "keys
            must be refreshed every N packets with cipher X".
\end{DoxyVerb}



\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\-S\-L configuration \\
\hline
{\em period} & The threshold value\-: a big-\/endian 64-\/bit number. Set to 2$^\wedge$64 -\/ 1 to disable periodic renegotiation \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a9a69464288d80b3904bc7540bd52aab0}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-session\-\_\-cache@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-session\-\_\-cache}}

\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-session\-\_\-cache}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-session\-\_\-cache (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-config} $\ast$}]{conf, }
\item[{void $\ast$}]{p\-\_\-cache, }
\item[{int($\ast$)(void $\ast$, {\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-session} $\ast$)}]{f\-\_\-get\-\_\-cache, }
\item[{int($\ast$)(void $\ast$, const {\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-session} $\ast$)}]{f\-\_\-set\-\_\-cache}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_a9a69464288d80b3904bc7540bd52aab0}


Set the session cache callbacks (server-\/side only) If not set, no session resuming is done (except if session tickets are enabled too). 

\begin{DoxyVerb}            The session cache has the responsibility to check for stale
            entries based on timeout. See RFC 5246 for recommendations.

            Warning: session.peer_cert is cleared by the SSL/TLS layer on
            connection shutdown, so do not cache the pointer! Either set
            it to NULL or make a full copy of the certificate.

            The get callback is called once during the initial handshake
            to enable session resuming. The get function has the
            following parameters: (void *parameter, mbedtls_ssl_session *session)
            If a valid entry is found, it should fill the master of
            the session object with the cached values and return 0,
            return 1 otherwise. Optionally peer_cert can be set as well
            if it is properly present in cache entry.

            The set callback is called once during the initial handshake
            to enable session resuming after the entire handshake has
            been finished. The set function has the following parameters:
            (void *parameter, const mbedtls_ssl_session *session). The function
            should create a cache entry for future retrieval based on
            the data in the session structure and should keep in mind
            that the mbedtls_ssl_session object presented (and all its referenced
            data) is cleared by the SSL/TLS layer when the connection is
            terminated. It is recommended to add metadata to determine if
            an entry is still valid in the future. Return 0 if
            successfully cached, return 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyVerb}



\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\-S\-L configuration \\
\hline
{\em p\-\_\-cache} & parmater (context) for both callbacks \\
\hline
{\em f\-\_\-get\-\_\-cache} & session get callback \\
\hline
{\em f\-\_\-set\-\_\-cache} & session set callback \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_a73725fed867e0fd29396c7c6565a76e6}


Set the allowed hashes for signatures during the handshake. (Default\-: all available hashes.) 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This only affects which hashes are offered and can be used for signatures during the handshake. Hashes for message authentication and the T\-L\-S P\-R\-F are controlled by the ciphersuite, see {\ttfamily \hyperlink{ssl_8h_ac8e4df37cadda8f743ed45501a51fec1}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-ciphersuites()}}. Hashes used for certificate signature are controlled by the verification profile, see {\ttfamily \hyperlink{ssl_8h_a35fde8579e1be441445daa09f8c639ed}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-cert\-\_\-profile()}}.

This list should be ordered by decreasing preference (preferred hash first).
\end{DoxyNote}

\hline
{\em hashes} & Ordered list of allowed signature hashes, terminated by {\ttfamily M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-M\-D\-\_\-\-N\-O\-N\-E}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a38ee2c1e3f232444df5ba3952d7ded33}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-sni@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-sni}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-sni@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-sni}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-sni}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-conf\-\_\-sni (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-config} $\ast$}]{conf, }
\item[{int($\ast$)(void $\ast$, {\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-context} $\ast$, const unsigned char $\ast$, size\-\_\-t)}]{f\-\_\-sni, }
\item[{void $\ast$}]{p\-\_\-sni}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_a38ee2c1e3f232444df5ba3952d7ded33}


Set server side Server\-Name T\-L\-S extension callback (optional, server-\/side only). 

\begin{DoxyVerb}            If set, the ServerName callback is called whenever the
            server receives a ServerName TLS extension from the client
            during a handshake. The ServerName callback has the
            following parameters: (void *parameter, mbedtls_ssl_context *ssl,
            const unsigned char *hostname, size_t len). If a suitable
            certificate is found, the callback must set the
            certificate(s) and key(s) to use with \c
            mbedtls_ssl_set_hs_own_cert() (can be called repeatedly),
            and may optionally adjust the CA and associated CRL with \c
            mbedtls_ssl_set_hs_ca_chain() as well as the client
            authentication mode with \c mbedtls_ssl_set_hs_authmode(),
            then must return 0. If no matching name is found, the
            callback must either set a default cert, or
            return non-zero to abort the handshake at this point.
\end{DoxyVerb}



\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\-S\-L configuration \\
\hline
{\em f\-\_\-sni} & verification function \\
\hline
{\em p\-\_\-sni} & verification parameter \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a4a37e497cd08c896870a42b1b618186e}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-handshake@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-handshake}}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-context} $\ast$}]{ssl}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_a4a37e497cd08c896870a42b1b618186e}


Perform the S\-S\-L handshake. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ssl} & S\-S\-L context\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-W\-A\-N\-T\-\_\-\-R\-E\-A\-D, M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-W\-A\-N\-T\-\_\-\-W\-R\-I\-T\-E, or a specific S\-S\-L error code.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If this function returns non-\/zero, then the ssl context becomes unusable, and you should either free it or call {\ttfamily \hyperlink{ssl_8h_a21432367cbce428f10dcb62d9456fa7e}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-session\-\_\-reset()}} on it before re-\/using it. If D\-T\-L\-S is in use, then you may choose to handle M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-H\-E\-L\-L\-O\-\_\-\-V\-E\-R\-I\-F\-Y\-\_\-\-R\-E\-Q\-U\-I\-R\-E\-D specially for logging purposes, but you still need to reset/free the context. 
\end{DoxyNote}

the number of bytes read, or 0 for E\-O\-F, or a negative error code. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Initiate an S\-S\-L renegotiation on the running connection. Client\-: perform the renegotiation right now. Server\-: request renegotiation, which will be performed during the next call to \hyperlink{ssl_8h_aa2c29eeb1deaf5ad9f01a7515006ede5}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-read()} if honored by client.

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, or any \hyperlink{ssl_8h_a4a37e497cd08c896870a42b1b618186e}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-handshake()} return value. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a143c1f887e1a2ca33b684ba4cf6c0543}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-set\-\_\-bio@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-set\-\_\-bio}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-set\-\_\-bio@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-set\-\_\-bio}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-set\-\_\-bio}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-set\-\_\-bio (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-context} $\ast$}]{ssl, }
\item[{void $\ast$}]{p\-\_\-bio, }
\item[{int($\ast$)(void $\ast$, const unsigned char $\ast$, size\-\_\-t)}]{f\-\_\-send, }
\item[{int($\ast$)(void $\ast$, unsigned char $\ast$, size\-\_\-t)}]{f\-\_\-recv, }
\item[{int($\ast$)(void $\ast$, unsigned char $\ast$, size\-\_\-t, uint32\-\_\-t)}]{f\-\_\-recv\-\_\-timeout}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_a143c1f887e1a2ca33b684ba4cf6c0543}


Set the underlying B\-I\-O callbacks for write, read and read-\/with-\/timeout. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ssl} & S\-S\-L context \\
\hline
{\em p\-\_\-bio} & parameter (context) shared by B\-I\-O callbacks \\
\hline
{\em f\-\_\-send} & write callback \\
\hline
{\em f\-\_\-recv} & read callback \\
\hline
{\em f\-\_\-recv\-\_\-timeout} & blocking read callback with timeout. The last argument is the timeout in milliseconds, 0 means no timeout (block forever until a message comes)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
One of f\-\_\-recv or f\-\_\-recv\-\_\-timeout can be N\-U\-L\-L, in which case the other is used. If both are non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L, f\-\_\-recv\-\_\-timeout is used and f\-\_\-recv is ignored (as if it were N\-U\-L\-L).

The two most common use cases are\-:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item non-\/blocking I/\-O, f\-\_\-recv != N\-U\-L\-L, f\-\_\-recv\-\_\-timeout == N\-U\-L\-L
\item blocking I/\-O, f\-\_\-recv == N\-U\-L\-L, f\-\_\-recv\-\_\-timout != N\-U\-L\-L
\end{DoxyItemize}

For D\-T\-L\-S, you need to provide either a non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L f\-\_\-recv\-\_\-timeout callback, or a f\-\_\-recv that doesn't block. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a15fab95c13a898f32fa69ff2065c1051}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-set\-\_\-client\-\_\-transport\-\_\-id@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-set\-\_\-client\-\_\-transport\-\_\-id}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-set\-\_\-client\-\_\-transport\-\_\-id@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-set\-\_\-client\-\_\-transport\-\_\-id}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-set\-\_\-client\-\_\-transport\-\_\-id}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-set\-\_\-client\-\_\-transport\-\_\-id (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{ilen}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_a15fab95c13a898f32fa69ff2065c1051}


Set client's transport-\/level identification info. (Server only. D\-T\-L\-S only.) 

\begin{DoxyVerb}            This is usually the IP address (and port), but could be
            anything identify the client depending on the underlying
            network stack. Used for HelloVerifyRequest with DTLS.
            This is *not* used to route the actual packets.
\end{DoxyVerb}



\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ssl} & S\-S\-L context \\
\hline
{\em info} & Transport-\/level info identifying the client (eg I\-P + port) \\
\hline
{\em ilen} & Length of info in bytes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
An internal copy is made, so the info buffer can be reused.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-B\-A\-D\-\_\-\-I\-N\-P\-U\-T\-\_\-\-D\-A\-T\-A if used on client, M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-A\-L\-L\-O\-C\-\_\-\-F\-A\-I\-L\-E\-D if out of memory. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\em p\-\_\-timer} & parameter (context) shared by timer callback \\
\hline
{\em f\-\_\-set\-\_\-timer} & set timer callback Accepts an intermediate and a final delay in milliseconcs If the final delay is 0, cancels the running timer. \\
\hline
{\em f\-\_\-get\-\_\-timer} & get timer callback. Must return\-: -\/1 if cancelled 0 if none of the delays is expired 1 if the intermediate delay only is expired 2 if the final delay is expired \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\hypertarget{ssl_8h_af79cb539a0ee6ac20cf9c574f4c3b343}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-setup@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-setup}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-setup@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-setup}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-setup}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-setup (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-context} $\ast$}]{ssl, }
\item[{const {\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-config} $\ast$}]{conf}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_af79cb539a0ee6ac20cf9c574f4c3b343}


Set up an S\-S\-L context for use. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
No copy of the configuration context is made, it can be shared by many \hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__context}{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-context} structures.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Modifying the conf structure after is has been used in this function is unsupported!
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ssl} & S\-S\-L context \\
\hline
{\em conf} & S\-S\-L configuration to use\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, or M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-A\-L\-L\-O\-C\-\_\-\-F\-A\-I\-L\-E\-D if memory allocation failed 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{ssl_8h_a5bbda87d484de82df730758b475f32e5}{\index{ssl.\-h@{ssl.\-h}!mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-write@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-write}}
\index{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-write@{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-write}!ssl.h@{ssl.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-write}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-write (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf mbedtls\-\_\-ssl\-\_\-context} $\ast$}]{ssl, }
\item[{const unsigned char $\ast$}]{buf, }
\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{len}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ssl_8h_a5bbda87d484de82df730758b475f32e5}


Write exactly 'len' application data bytes. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ssl} & S\-S\-L context \\
\hline
{\em buf} & buffer holding the data \\
\hline
{\em len} & how many bytes must be written\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the number of bytes written, or a negative error code.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
When this function returns M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-W\-A\-N\-T\-\_\-\-W\-R\-I\-T\-E, it must be called later with the {\itshape same} arguments, until it returns a positive value.

If the requested length is greater than the maximum fragment length (either the built-\/in limit or the one set or negotiated with the peer), then\-:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item with T\-L\-S, less bytes than requested are written. (In order to write larger messages, this function should be called in a loop.)
\item with D\-T\-L\-S, M\-B\-E\-D\-T\-L\-S\-\_\-\-E\-R\-R\-\_\-\-S\-S\-L\-\_\-\-B\-A\-D\-\_\-\-I\-N\-P\-U\-T\-\_\-\-D\-A\-T\-A is returned. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}
